<a name="introduction"></a> <span data-ttu-id="61b48-103">Bu makaledeki tablolar, artık kullanılmayan türler listesinde [!INCLUDE[net_v45](../../../includes/net-v45-md.md)] ve [!INCLUDE[net_v46](../../../includes/net-v46-md.md)], derleme tarafından düzenlenmiş.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="61b48-103">The tables in this article list the types that are obsolete in the [!INCLUDE[net_v45](../../../includes/net-v45-md.md)] and the [!INCLUDE[net_v46](../../../includes/net-v46-md.md)], organized by assembly.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="61b48-104">Eski türler ve önerilen alternatifleri her derlemede bir listesini görmek için aşağıdaki bağlantıları kullanın.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="61b48-104">Use the following links to see a list of the obsolete types and the recommended alternatives in each assembly.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="61b48-105">Bu tür geçersiz olduğundan, tüm üyeleri de artık kullanılmıyor.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="61b48-105">Because these types are obsolete, all their members are also obsolete.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="61b48-106">.NET Framework Sınıf Kitaplığı'nda ek eski üyeler listesi için bkz. [eski üyeler](../../../docs/framework/whats-new/obsolete-members.md).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="61b48-106">For a list of additional obsolete members in the .NET Framework class library, see [Obsolete Members](../../../docs/framework/whats-new/obsolete-members.md).</span></span>
